msg:Although I only stayed for one night, I will definitely stay in this hotel again next time I come to Guangzhou. The hotel is in the Design City, next to the Yunmen Shopping Mall, and there are many choices for shopping and dining. There are also various snacks around the hotel, Luckin Coffee, and you can walk to the hotel from Exit D of Huangbian Station on Metro Line 2. The hotel's buffet breakfast is also very good, with authentic Cantonese dim sum. The chef will provide guests with various types of porridge, noodles, and noodles according to your favorite side dishes. If you are hungry at night and want to order takeout, the hotel robot can also provide food delivery to your room. From the entrance of the hotel, every staff member you meet will take the initiative to greet the guests. The front desk lady will provide guests with WeChat and provide guests with high-quality and efficient services 24 hours a day! I also like the design in the room, which is simple, stylish and generous. The bed is also very comfortable, the shower head water is very large, and the air conditioning cooling effect is also good! Compared with some famous five-star hotels, Junya's hardware facilities are still worthy of praise! The only shortcoming during this stay is that it is a bit inconvenient for motor vehicles to enter and exit. Because of construction, motor vehicles are not allowed to pass through the design park. Sometimes the driver who calls a car is afraid of trouble and does not want to drive to the underground parking lot. You need to walk to the park gate to get a car. I hope that the park will allow cars to pass through next time I stay. Overall, the stay experience was great and it is definitely worth recommending to friends!
